***извернуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извернуться.html>изверну́ться</a> (25684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извернуться.html>изверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изворачиваться.html>извора́чиваться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">извёртываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn sharply</li>
<li>to twist deftly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to accomplish or avoid something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find a way out of a predicament, to be resourceful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try to get rid of something unpleasant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use cunning or trickery, to contrive</li></ol>

***извести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести</a> (15532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to use up, to spend</li>
<li>to exterminate</li>
<li>to exhaust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvestí</b> sebjá rabótoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overwork oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to torment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvestí</b> nasméškami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bait</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to vex, to exasperate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvestí</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative perfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ízvestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

***известковый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:известковый.html>известко́вый</a> (21803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известка.html>извёстка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvjóstka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известковый.html>известко́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvestkóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lime, quicklime
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:известковый.html>известко́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvestkóvoje</b> molokó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">milk of lime</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> limestone</li>
<li>paper-white, pale</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стность</a> (8279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvéstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvéstnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>reputation, fame, repute, notoriety, renown</li>
<li>publicity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> celebrity, prominent figure, notability</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvéstnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изве́стнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изве́стней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известнейший.html>изве́стнейший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>known, familiar</li>
<li>well-known, renowned, famous</li>
<li>notorious</li>
<li>certain</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄσβεστος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ásbestos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ízvestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>и́звести</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>и́звести</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звестей</a></b>)

<ol><li>lime <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">calcium oxide, quicklime</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гашёная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gašónaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slaked lime, slack lime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">негашёная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">negašónaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quicklime, burnt lime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">хло́рная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xlórnaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">chloride of lime, bleaching powder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извещать.html>извеща́ть</a> (15682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извещать.html>извеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izveščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inform, to notify, to give notice</li>
<li>to announce, to advertise</li></ol>

***извиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a> (9186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виться.html>ви́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изви́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to coil, to wriggle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvivátʹsja</b> ot bóli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to writhe with pain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(river, road etc)</i> to twist, to wind, to meander</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извиниться.html>извини́ться</a> (6064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***извлекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a> (7912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">извле́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvlék-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvlekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extract, to elicit, to draw out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> štó-libo iz čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive something from something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> urók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn a lesson (from); to moralize, to draw the moral</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льзу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> pólʹzu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive benefit (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>при́были</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> ogrómnyje príbyli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive / make huge profits (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> udovólʹstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive pleasure (from)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извлекаться.html>извлека́ться</a> (28922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvléčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extract, to elicit, to draw out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvléčʹ</b> urók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn a lesson (from); to moralize, to draw the moral</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льзу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvléčʹ</b> pólʹzu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive benefit (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>при́были</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvléčʹ</b> ogrómnyje príbyli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive / make huge profits (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvléčʹ</b> udovólʹstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive pleasure (from)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***извне.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извне.html>извне</a> (9282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извне.html>извне́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvné</span>)
</p>
